## 1\. ä»€ä¹ˆæ˜¯ Reactive åˆçº¦ï¼Ÿ

## 3\. å®æˆ˜éƒ¨ç½² (Foundry ç¯å¢ƒ)

### Step 1. ç¯å¢ƒåˆå§‹åŒ–

å…‹éš†ä»“åº“å¹¶åŠ è½½ä¾èµ–ï¼š

### Step 2. å…³é”®ç¯å¢ƒå˜é‡é…ç½® (`.env`)

> **æ³¨æ„**ï¼šç”±äº Lasna ç½‘ç»œå‡çº§ï¼Œå¿…é¡»ä½¿ç”¨æœ€æ–°çš„ `rnk.dev` åŸŸåã€‚

| å˜é‡å | æ¨èå€¼/è¯´æ˜ | | ORIGIN\_RPC | Sepolia Infura/Alchemy URL | | REACTIVE\_RPC | [https://lasna-rpc.rnk.dev/](https://lasna-rpc.rnk.dev/) | | SYSTEM\_CONTRACT\_ADDR | 0x0000000000000000000000000000000000fffFfF | | DESTINATION\_CALLBACK\_PROXY\_ADDR | 0xc9f36411C9897e7F959D99ffca2a0Ba7ee0D7bDA |

### Step 3. éƒ¨ç½²æµç¨‹å‘½ä»¤

1.  **æºåˆçº¦**ï¼š`forge create --rpc-url $ORIGIN_RPC --private-key $PRIVATE_KEY src/demos/basic/BasicDemoL1Contract.sol:BasicDemoL1Contract`
    
2.  **å›è°ƒåˆçº¦**ï¼š`forge create --rpc-url $DESTINATION_RPC --private-key $PRIVATE_KEY src/demos/basic/BasicDemoL1Callback.sol:BasicDemoL1Callback --value 0.02ether --constructor-args $DESTINATION_CALLBACK_PROXY_ADDR`
    
3.  **Reactive åˆçº¦**ï¼šä½¿ç”¨ `11155111` (Sepolia ID) å’Œ `0x8cab...` (Event Hash) ä½œä¸ºæ„é€ å‚æ•°ã€‚

## 4\. Debug Logs

åœ¨æœ¬æ¬¡å®æˆ˜ä¸­ï¼Œä¸¤ä¸ªé‡å¤§ç½‘ç»œæŠ€æœ¯éšœç¢ï¼š

### é—®é¢˜ 1ï¼šTLS Handshake EOF / OS Error 10053

-   **ç°è±¡**ï¼šè®¿é—® `kopernikus.reactive.network` æ—¶æŠ¥é”™ï¼Œæ¡æ‰‹è¢«å¼ºåˆ¶ä¸­æ–­ã€‚
    
-   **å¯¹ç­–**ï¼š
    
    -   **æ›´æ¢ RPC**ï¼šä½¿ç”¨äº†æœ€æ–°çš„ Lasna å®˜æ–¹ RPC `https://lasna-rpc.rnk.dev/`ã€‚

é“¾ä¸Šæ—¥å¿—æ˜¯è§£ç  Polymarket æ•°æ®çš„æ ¸å¿ƒï¼ŒConditionPreparation ç¡®è®¤å¸‚åœºåŸºç¡€ä¿¡æ¯ï¼ŒPositionSplit ä¸ PositionsMerge è®°å½•å¤´å¯¸çš„ç”Ÿæˆä¸é”€æ¯ï¼ŒOrderFilled è¿˜åŸäº¤æ˜“è¯¦æƒ…ï¼Œè¿™äº›æ—¥å¿—ä¸²è”å½¢æˆå®Œæ•´è¯æ®é“¾ï¼Œæ”¯æŒé€šè¿‡äº¤æ˜“å“ˆå¸Œè§£æäº¤æ˜“ç»†èŠ‚ã€é€šè¿‡ conditionId è¿˜åŸå¸‚åœºå‚æ•°ï¼Œå®ç°å¯¹å¸‚åœºå…¨æµç¨‹çš„è¿½æº¯ä¸éªŒè¯ã€‚

## äºŒã€ä»»åŠ¡Aï¼šPolymarket äº¤æ˜“è§£ç å™¨

å®ç°ä¸€ä¸ªé€šç”¨çš„äº¤æ˜“æ—¥å¿—è§£æå™¨ï¼Œè¾“å…¥äº¤æ˜“å“ˆå¸Œï¼ˆåœ¨ Polygon é“¾ä¸Šï¼‰ï¼Œè¾“å‡ºè¯¥äº¤æ˜“ä¸­ Polymarket è®¢å•æ’®åˆçš„è¯¦æƒ…ã€‚

å®Œæ•´çš„å®ç°ä»£ç ï¼Œè¯·è®¿é—®æˆ‘çš„ GitHub ä»“åº“[SU-AN-coder/â€“A](https://github.com/SU-AN-coder/--A)

### ä¸€ã€ æ ¸å¿ƒæŠ€æœ¯æŒ‘æˆ˜ä¸é”™è¯¯åˆ†æ

**1\. èŠ‚ç‚¹é€šè®¯ç“¶é¢ˆï¼š**`ExtraDataLengthError`

-   **é‡åˆ°çš„é”™è¯¯**ï¼šåœ¨ä½¿ç”¨ `web3.py` è¿æ¥ Polygon èŠ‚ç‚¹æ—¶ï¼Œç¨‹åºé¢‘ç¹æŠ›å‡ºâ€œåŒºå—å¤´ extraData é•¿åº¦è¶…æ ‡â€çš„å¼‚å¸¸ã€‚
    
-   **æŠ€æœ¯åŸå› **ï¼šä»¥å¤ªåŠæ ‡å‡†è§„å®š `extraData` é•¿åº¦ä¸º 32 å­—èŠ‚ã€‚ä½† Polygon é‡‡ç”¨ **PoA (Proof of Authority)** å…±è¯†ï¼Œä¸ºäº†å®‰å…¨æ€§ï¼ŒéªŒè¯è€…çš„ç­¾åè¢«å¼ºåˆ¶å¡è¿›äº†è¿™ä¸ªå­—æ®µï¼Œå¯¼è‡´å…¶é•¿åº¦è¿œè¶…æ ‡å‡†ã€‚
    
-   **è§£å†³æ–¹æ¡ˆ**ï¼šé€šè¿‡æ³¨å…¥ç‰¹å®šçš„ä¸­é—´ä»¶æ¥â€œåŠ«æŒâ€è¯·æ±‚ï¼Œå‘Šè¯‰åº“å¦‚ä½•å¤„ç†éæ ‡çš„åŒºå—ç»“æ„ã€‚

**2\. å¼‚æ­¥æ•°æ®ä¸åŒæ­¥ï¼š**`Transaction Not Found`

-   **é‡åˆ°çš„é”™è¯¯**ï¼šåœ¨åŒºå—é“¾æµè§ˆå™¨ï¼ˆPolygonscanï¼‰ä¸Šå·²ç»ç¡®è®¤æˆäº¤çš„äº¤æ˜“ï¼Œé€šè¿‡ RPC æ¥å£æŸ¥è¯¢å´è¿”å›â€œæ‰¾ä¸åˆ°äº¤æ˜“â€ã€‚
    
-   **æŠ€æœ¯åŸå› **ï¼šå…¬å…± RPC èŠ‚ç‚¹ï¼ˆå¦‚ `drpc`ï¼‰å®é™…ä¸Šæ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªèŠ‚ç‚¹é›†ç¾¤ã€‚å½“ä½ å‘èµ·è¯·æ±‚æ—¶ï¼Œå¯èƒ½ä¼šè¢«åˆ†é…åˆ°å°šæœªå®Œæˆæœ€æ–°å—åŒæ­¥çš„æœåŠ¡å™¨ä¸Šã€‚
    
-   **ä¼˜åŒ–ç­–ç•¥**ï¼šå¼•å…¥äº† **å¤‡ç”¨èŠ‚ç‚¹æ± ** å’Œ **æŒ‡æ•°é€€é¿é‡è¯•æœºåˆ¶**ã€‚å½“ä¸»èŠ‚ç‚¹è¿”å›ç©ºå€¼æ—¶ï¼Œè„šæœ¬ä¼šè‡ªåŠ¨è½®è¯¢å…¶ä»–æœåŠ¡å•†ã€‚
    

### äºŒã€ å…³é”®æŠ€æœ¯ï¼šEVM æ—¥å¿—çš„â€œå‰¥ç¦»â€ä¸â€œåˆ‡ç‰‡â€

Polymarket çš„æˆäº¤æ•°æ®å¹¶ä¸æ˜¯æ˜æ–‡ï¼Œè€Œæ˜¯å­˜å‚¨åœ¨ `receipt['logs']` é‡Œçš„åå…­è¿›åˆ¶å­—èŠ‚æµä¸­ã€‚

**1\. Topic è·¯ç”±è¿‡æ»¤**

ä¸ºäº†åœ¨æˆåƒä¸Šä¸‡çš„æ—¥å¿—ä¸­æ‰¾åˆ°é‚£ä¸€ç¬”æˆäº¤ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬ä½¿ç”¨äº† **Event Signatureï¼ˆäº‹ä»¶ç­¾åï¼‰** æŠ€æœ¯ã€‚

-   `OrderFilled` äº‹ä»¶çš„å”¯ä¸€æ ‡è¯†ç¬¦ï¼ˆTopic\[0\]ï¼‰æ˜¯å…¶å‡½æ•°ç­¾åçš„ Keccak-256 å“ˆå¸Œå€¼ï¼š`0x3445565da59ada415359f99440a7800906b948a74999f17666f4e7f3e547c133`ã€‚
    
-   ç¨‹åºåªå¤„ç†å‘½ä¸­è¯¥å“ˆå¸Œä¸”æ¥æºäº Polymarket äº¤æ˜“æ‰€åˆçº¦åœ°å€ï¼ˆ`0x4bFb...`ï¼‰çš„æ—¥å¿—ã€‚
    

**2\. Data å­—æ®µçš„åˆ‡ç‰‡è§£ç  (Hex Slicing)**

è¿™æ˜¯æœ€ç¡¬æ ¸çš„éƒ¨åˆ†ã€‚`Data` å­—æ®µæ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªå·¨å¤§çš„åå…­è¿›åˆ¶é•¿ä¸²ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬å¿…é¡»å°†å…¶æŒ‰æ¯ **32 å­—èŠ‚ï¼ˆ64 ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦ï¼‰** è¿›è¡Œç‰©ç†åˆ‡ç‰‡ï¼š

Python

```

# æ¯ 64 ä½æˆªå–ä¸€ä¸ªå‚æ•°

```

### ä¸‰ã€ ä¸šåŠ¡é€»è¾‘åˆ¤å®šï¼šå¦‚ä½•è¯†åˆ«â€œä¹°â€ä¸â€œå–â€

åœ¨é“¾ä¸Šï¼Œæ‰€æœ‰çš„ä»£å¸éƒ½æ˜¯ ID

-   **åˆ¤å®šæ ‡å‡†**ï¼šPolymarket è§„å®š USDC çš„ `AssetId` æ°¸è¿œä¸º `0`ã€‚
    
-   **BUY é€»è¾‘**ï¼šå¦‚æœ `makerAssetId == 0`ï¼Œä»£è¡¨æŒ‚å•äººæä¾›çš„æ˜¯é’±ï¼Œåƒå•äººæä¾›çš„æ˜¯ Tokenã€‚
    
-   **ä»·æ ¼è®¡ç®—**ï¼šé€šè¿‡ `(æ”¯ä»˜çš„USDCæ•°é‡ / è·å¾—çš„Tokenæ•°é‡)` è¿˜åŸå‡ºç”¨æˆ·åœ¨å‰ç«¯çœ‹åˆ°çš„æˆäº¤å•ä»·ï¼ˆä¾‹å¦‚ 0.52 USDCï¼‰ã€‚
    

### å››ã€ æˆæœï¼šæ ‡å‡†åŒ–çš„ JSON è¾“å‡º

æœ€ç»ˆï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬å°†å¤æ‚çš„åŸå§‹å­—èŠ‚æµè½¬åŒ–ä¸ºäº†ç¬¦åˆä»»åŠ¡ A è¦æ±‚çš„ç»“æ„åŒ–æ•°æ®ã€‚

![å±å¹•æˆªå›¾ 2026-01-22 164342.png](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/IntensiveCoLearning/Web3_Internship_Bootcamp_2026_Winter/main/assets/SU-AN-coder/images/2026-01-23-1769158750332-_____2026-01-22_164342.png)

## ä¸‰ã€ä»»åŠ¡Bï¼šå¸‚åœºå‚æ•°è§£ç  (Market Decoder)

ç»™å®šé“¾ä¸Šè·å–çš„å¸‚åœºåˆ›å»ºç›¸å…³ä¿¡æ¯ï¼ˆå¦‚ `ConditionPreparation` æ—¥å¿—ï¼Œæˆ–å·²çŸ¥çš„ `conditionId`ï¼‰ï¼Œæå–å¹¶è®¡ç®—å‡ºè¯¥å¸‚åœºçš„æ ¸å¿ƒé“¾ä¸Šå‚æ•°ï¼ŒåŒ…æ‹¬é¢„è¨€æœºã€é—®é¢˜ IDã€æŠµæŠ¼å“åœ°å€ï¼Œä»¥åŠ YES/NO ä¸¤ç§å¤´å¯¸çš„ TokenId

å®Œæ•´çš„å®ç°ä»£ç ï¼Œè¯·è®¿é—®æˆ‘çš„ GitHub ä»“åº“[SU-AN-coder/market-b](https://github.com/SU-AN-coder/market-b)

### 1\. æ ¸å¿ƒæŠ€æœ¯åŸç†ï¼šæ¡ä»¶ä»£å¸æ¡†æ¶ (CTF)

Polymarket çš„åº•å±‚æ˜¯ **Gnosis Conditional Tokens Framework (CTF)**ã€‚å…¶æ ¸å¿ƒé€»è¾‘æ˜¯å°†ç°å®ä¸–ç•Œçš„é—®é¢˜ï¼ˆOracle + QuestionIdï¼‰è½¬åŒ–ä¸ºé“¾ä¸Šå¯äº¤æ˜“çš„èµ„äº§ã€‚

ä»æŠ€æœ¯å®ç°ä¸Šï¼Œè¿™æ¶‰åŠåˆ°ä¸€ä¸ª**åµŒå¥—å“ˆå¸Œ**çš„è®¡ç®—è¿‡ç¨‹ï¼š

-   **Collection ID çš„ç”Ÿæˆ**ï¼šå®ƒå¹¶ä¸æ˜¯éšæœºç”Ÿæˆçš„ UUIDï¼Œè€Œæ˜¯é€šè¿‡ `keccak256` å“ˆå¸Œè®¡ç®—å¾—å‡ºçš„ã€‚æŠ€æœ¯ç»†èŠ‚åœ¨äºå®ƒç»‘å®šäº† `conditionId` å’Œä¸€ä¸ª `indexSet`ï¼ˆä½æ©ç ï¼‰ã€‚
    
    -   **æŠ€æœ¯å‘ç‚¹**ï¼šåœ¨ Python å®ç°ä¸­ï¼Œ`indexSet` å¿…é¡»è¢«å¤„ç†ä¸º `bytes32`ï¼ˆ32å­—èŠ‚å¤§ç«¯åºï¼‰ã€‚å¦‚æœç›´æ¥æŒ‰æ™®é€šæ•´æ•°å¤„ç†ï¼Œç®—å‡ºæ¥çš„å“ˆå¸Œå€¼ä¼šå®Œå…¨å¯¹ä¸ä¸Šã€‚
        
-   **Position ID (TokenID) çš„é”šå®š**ï¼šè¿™æ˜¯æœ€ç»ˆåœ¨ ERC-1155 åˆçº¦ä¸­æµè½¬çš„ IDã€‚å®ƒæ˜¯å°† `collateralToken`ï¼ˆæŠµæŠ¼å“åœ°å€ï¼‰ä¸ä¸Šè¿° `Collection ID` å†æ¬¡è¿›è¡Œå“ˆå¸Œçš„ç»“æœã€‚
    

### 2\. é‡åˆ°çš„æŠ€æœ¯é—®é¢˜

A. ç¯å¢ƒå˜é‡ä¸æ“ä½œç³»ç»Ÿçš„å·®å¼‚

åœ¨ Windows PowerShell ç¯å¢ƒä¸‹è¿è¡Œ Python è„šæœ¬æ—¶ï¼ŒLinux é£æ ¼çš„æ¢è¡Œç¬¦ `\` ä¼šå¯¼è‡´è§£æé”™è¯¯ã€‚

-   ç°è±¡ï¼šå‡ºç° `MissingExpressionAfterOperator` æŠ¥é”™ã€‚
    
-   è§£å†³æ–¹æ¡ˆï¼šè¿™æ˜¯ç”±äº PowerShell å°† `--` è¯¯è®¤ä¸ºæ˜¯å‡æ³•è¿ç®—ç¬¦ã€‚åœ¨ç¼–å†™è·¨å¹³å°å·¥å…·æ—¶ï¼Œå¿…é¡»è€ƒè™‘åˆ° Shell ç¯å¢ƒå¯¹å‚æ•°è§£æçš„æ•æ„Ÿæ€§ã€‚æ¨èåœ¨æ–‡æ¡£ä¸­æä¾›**å•è¡Œå‘½ä»¤**æˆ–ä½¿ç”¨åå¼•å· `` ` `` ä½œä¸ºæ¢è¡Œç¬¦ã€‚
    

B. æ•°æ®ç±»å‹çš„ä¸¥è°¨ (ABI Encoding)

åœ¨è®¡ç®—å“ˆå¸Œä¹‹å‰ï¼Œå¿…é¡»æ¨¡æ‹Ÿ EVM çš„å†…å­˜å¸ƒå±€ã€‚

-   **ç»†èŠ‚**ï¼šæŠµæŠ¼å“åœ°å€ï¼ˆAddressï¼‰æ˜¯ 20 å­—èŠ‚ï¼Œä½†åœ¨å“ˆå¸Œè®¡ç®—ä¸­ï¼Œå®ƒé€šå¸¸éœ€è¦è¢«å·¦è¡¥é›¶ï¼ˆLeft Paddingï¼‰è‡³ 32 å­—èŠ‚ã€‚
    
-   **ä»£ç ç‰‡æ®µç¤ºä¾‹**ï¼š
    
    Python
    
    ```
    # å…³é”®ç‚¹ï¼šå°† 20 å­—èŠ‚åœ°å€è½¬æ¢ä¸º 32 å­—èŠ‚ bytes æ ¼å¼
    collateral_bytes = to_bytes(hexstr=address).rjust(32, b'\x00')
    ```
    
    psï¼šå¦‚æœä¸åšè¿™ä¸ªè¡¥é½æ“ä½œï¼Œç®—å‡ºæ¥çš„ `tokenId` ä¼šä¸é“¾ä¸Šå®é™… ID äº§ç”Ÿâ€œå·®ä¹‹æ¯«å˜ï¼Œè°¬ä»¥åƒé‡Œâ€çš„ç»“æœ
    

### 3\. æ•°æ®ä¸€è‡´æ€§æ ¡éªŒ (Verification)

ä¸€ä¸ªå¥å£®çš„è§£ç å™¨ä¸èƒ½åªé¡¾ç€ç®—ï¼Œè¿˜å¾—å…·å¤‡**è‡ªæˆ‘éªŒè¯**çš„èƒ½åŠ›ã€‚æˆ‘ä»¬å¼•å…¥äº†ä¸¤ä¸ªç»´åº¦çš„æ ¡éªŒï¼š

1.  **Gamma API äº¤å‰å¼•ç”¨**ï¼š Polymarket å®˜æ–¹çš„ Gamma API ä¼šæä¾› `clobTokenIds`ã€‚æˆ‘ä»¬çš„è§£ç å™¨è¾“å‡ºå¿…é¡»ä¸ä¹‹ 100% åŒ¹é…ã€‚è¿™æ˜¯éªŒè¯æˆ‘ä»¬å“ˆå¸Œç®—æ³•æ˜¯å¦è¿‡æ—¶çš„â€œé‡‘æ ‡å‡†â€ã€‚
    
2.  **äº¤æ˜“æµé—­ç¯**ï¼š åœ¨è§£æ `OrderFilled`ï¼ˆè®¢å•æˆäº¤ï¼‰æ—¥å¿—æ—¶ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬ä¼šæå–å…¶ä¸­çš„èµ„äº§ IDã€‚é€šè¿‡ Market Decoderï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬å¯ä»¥ç¬é—´åˆ¤å®šè¿™ç¬”äº¤æ˜“æ˜¯åœ¨å“ªä¸ªç»†åˆ†å¸‚åœºï¼ˆConditionï¼‰ä¸‹å‘ç”Ÿçš„ï¼Œä»è€Œå®ç°ä»â€œé“¾ä¸Šå™ªéŸ³â€åˆ°â€œç»“æ„åŒ–ä¿¡æ¯â€çš„è½¬åŒ–ã€‚

## äºŒã€å¼€å‘å‡†å¤‡

## ä¸‰ã€å¼€å‘è¿‡ç¨‹ï¼ˆé—®é¢˜ - å°è¯• - è§£å†³ï¼‰

### é˜¶æ®µ 1ï¼šåˆå§‹å°è¯• - ç›´æ¥ä½¿ç”¨ SpoonOS SDK

**é—®é¢˜ï¼šæ¨¡å‹å¼ºåˆ¶å›é€€æŠ¥é”™**

ä»£ç å°è¯•ï¼šç›´æ¥å®ä¾‹åŒ– SpoonReactAI ç±»ï¼ŒæŒ‡å®šè±†åŒ…æ¨¡å‹ ID å’Œ API å¯†é’¥ï¼š

```
    tools=[RealTimePriceTool()],
    model=model_id,
    api_key=api_key,
    base_url=base_url

```

æŠ¥é”™ä¿¡æ¯ï¼š`[openai] Model 'gpt-4.1' not found or not available`

åŸå› åˆ†æï¼šSpoonOS SDK å†…éƒ¨æœ‰ç¡¬ç¼–ç æ ¡éªŒï¼ŒAPI Key é `sk-` å¼€å¤´ï¼ˆOpenAI æ ¼å¼ï¼‰æ—¶ï¼Œä¼šè‡ªåŠ¨å›é€€åˆ°é»˜è®¤çš„ `gpt-4.1` æ¨¡å‹ï¼Œè€Œè¯¥æ¨¡å‹ä¸å­˜åœ¨ã€‚

**å°è¯• 1ï¼šçŒ´å­è¡¥ä¸ï¼ˆMonkey Patchï¼‰å¼ºåˆ¶ä¿®æ”¹é…ç½®**

æ ¸å¿ƒæ€è·¯ï¼šè¿è¡Œæ—¶ä¿®æ”¹ Agent ç±»çš„é…ç½®å±æ€§ï¼Œæ›¿æ¢æ¨¡å‹ IDï¼š

python

```
# éå†Agentå±æ€§ï¼Œå¼ºåˆ¶ä¿®æ­£æ¨¡å‹é…ç½®
for attr in dir(agent):
    if "config" in attr.lower() and isinstance(getattr(agent, attr), dict):
        getattr(agent, attr)["model"] = model_id
# è¦†ç›–llmå¯¹è±¡çš„é…ç½®

```

ç»“æœï¼šä¾ç„¶æŠ¥é”™ï¼ŒSDK åº•å±‚é—­åŒ… / ç§æœ‰å˜é‡æœªè¢«ä¿®æ”¹ï¼Œè¿è¡Œæ—¶ä»è¯»å–é»˜è®¤é…ç½®ã€‚

å°è¯• 2ï¼šä¿®æ”¹ API Key æ ¼å¼ï¼ˆè¸©å‘ï¼‰

-   é”™è¯¯æ“ä½œï¼šæ‰‹åŠ¨ç»™è±†åŒ… API Key åŠ  `sk-` å‰ç¼€ï¼Œè¯•å›¾éª—è¿‡ SDK æ ¡éªŒã€‚
    
-   æ–°æŠ¥é”™ï¼š`[openai] Authentication failed - check API key`
    
-   åŸå› ï¼šè±†åŒ…é‰´æƒä¸è¯†åˆ« `sk-` å‰ç¼€ï¼ŒåŸç”Ÿ UUID æ ¼å¼æ‰æœ‰æ•ˆï¼ŒSDK æ ¡éªŒä¸è±†åŒ…é‰´æƒè§„åˆ™å†²çªã€‚
    

### é˜¶æ®µ 2ï¼šç ´å±€ - åè®®é‡æ„ï¼Œç»•è¿‡ SDK å°è£…

æ ¸å¿ƒæ€è·¯ï¼š

æ”¾å¼ƒ SpoonOS çš„é«˜å±‚ `SpoonReactAI` å°è£…ï¼Œä¿ç•™å…¶å·¥å…·å®šä¹‰è§„èŒƒï¼ˆPydantic é©±åŠ¨ï¼‰ï¼Œç›´æ¥é€šè¿‡ OpenAI å…¼å®¹åè®®å¯¹æ¥è±†åŒ…ï¼Œæ‰‹åŠ¨å®ç° ReAct å¾ªç¯ã€‚

æ­¥éª¤ 1ï¼šå®šä¹‰å·¥å…·åŠå‚æ•° Schema

ç”¨ Pydantic å®šä¹‰å·¥å…·å‚æ•°ï¼Œè‡ªåŠ¨ç”Ÿæˆæ¨¡å‹å¯è¯†åˆ«çš„ JSON Schemaï¼š

python

è¿è¡Œ

```
from pydantic import BaseModel, Field
from tools import RealTimePriceTool, SpoonSwapTool

# ä»·æ ¼æŸ¥è¯¢å·¥å…·å‚æ•°å®šä¹‰
class PriceArgs(BaseModel):
    symbol: str = Field(description="ä»£å¸ç¬¦å·ï¼Œä¾‹å¦‚ ETH æˆ– BTC")

# äº¤æ˜“å·¥å…·å‚æ•°å®šä¹‰
class SwapArgs(BaseModel):
    token_in: str = Field(description="å¾…å–å‡ºçš„ä»£å¸ç¬¦å·")
    amount: float = Field(description="å–å‡ºæ•°é‡")

# åˆå§‹åŒ–å·¥å…·å®ä¾‹
price_tool = RealTimePriceTool()
swap_tool = SpoonSwapTool()
```

æ­¥éª¤ 2ï¼šæ‰‹åŠ¨æ„å»º ReAct å¾ªç¯

python

```
import asyncio
from openai import AsyncOpenAI
import json

async def main():
    # åˆå§‹åŒ–è±†åŒ…å®¢æˆ·ç«¯ï¼ˆå…¼å®¹OpenAIåè®®ï¼‰
    client = AsyncOpenAI(
        api_key=os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY"),
        base_url=os.getenv("OPENAI_BASE_URL")
    )

    # æ„å»ºå·¥å…·æè¿°ï¼Œè®©æ¨¡å‹ç†è§£å¯ç”¨å·¥å…·
    tools_definition = [
        {
            "type": "function",
            "function": {
                "name": price_tool.name,
                "description": price_tool.description,
                "parameters": PriceArgs.model_json_schema()
            }
        },
        {
            "type": "function",
            "function": {
                "name": swap_tool.name,
                "description": swap_tool.description,
                "parameters": SwapArgs.model_json_schema()
            }
        }
    ]

    # ç”¨æˆ·æŒ‡ä»¤
    messages = [
        {"role": "system", "content": "ä½ æ˜¯åŠ å¯†è´§å¸äº¤æ˜“åŠ©æ‰‹ï¼Œéœ€è°ƒç”¨å·¥å…·å®Œæˆç”¨æˆ·æŒ‡ä»¤"},
        {"role": "user", "content": "æŸ¥è¯¢ETHå½“å‰ä»·æ ¼ï¼Œä½äº4000ç¾å…ƒåˆ™æ¨¡æ‹Ÿä¹°å…¥0.5ä¸ª"}
    ]

    # 1. æ¨¡å‹å†³ç­–ï¼šæ˜¯å¦è°ƒç”¨å·¥å…·
    response = await client.chat.completions.create(
        model=os.getenv("DOUBAO_ENDPOINT_ID"),
        messages=messages,
        tools=tools_definition,
        tool_choice="auto"
    )

    # 2. æ‰§è¡Œå·¥å…·è°ƒç”¨
    response_message = response.choices[0].message
    if response_message.tool_calls:
        for tool_call in response_message.tool_calls:
            func_name = tool_call.function.name
            args = json.loads(tool_call.function.arguments)
            # å·¥å…·åˆ†å‘æ‰§è¡Œ
            if func_name == "get_token_price":
                result = price_tool.execute(**args)
            elif func_name == "execute_swap":
                result = swap_tool.execute(**args)
            print(f"å·¥å…·æ‰§è¡Œç»“æœï¼š{result}")
```

ç»“æœï¼šæˆåŠŸè·‘é€šï¼æ¨¡å‹èƒ½æ­£ç¡®è¯†åˆ«å·¥å…·ã€ä¼ é€’å‚æ•°ï¼Œå·¥å…·æ‰§è¡Œåè¿”å›ç»“æœï¼Œå®ç°å®Œæ•´æ™ºèƒ½å¾ªç¯ã€‚

## å››ã€æœ€ç»ˆæˆæœ

1.  åŠŸèƒ½å®ç°ï¼š
    
    -   å®æ—¶ä»·æ ¼æŸ¥è¯¢ï¼šè°ƒç”¨ `RealTimePriceTool` è·å– ETH/BTC ç­‰ä»£å¸ä»·æ ¼ï¼›
        
    -   æ™ºèƒ½å†³ç­–ï¼šè±†åŒ…æ¨¡å‹æ ¹æ®ä»·æ ¼åˆ¤æ–­æ˜¯å¦è§¦å‘äº¤æ˜“æ¡ä»¶ï¼›
        
    -   æ¨¡æ‹Ÿäº¤æ˜“ï¼šæ»¡è¶³æ¡ä»¶æ—¶æ‰§è¡Œ `SpoonSwapTool` æ¨¡æ‹Ÿä¹°å…¥ / å–å‡ºã€‚
        
2.  ä»£ç ç»“æ„ï¼š
    
    -   `main.py`ï¼šæ ¸å¿ƒ ReAct å¾ªç¯ã€æ¨¡å‹å¯¹æ¥ã€å·¥å…·è°ƒåº¦ï¼›
        
    -   `tools.py`ï¼šä»·æ ¼æŸ¥è¯¢ã€äº¤æ˜“æ¨¡æ‹Ÿå·¥å…·å®ç°ï¼›
        
    -   `.env.example`ï¼šç¯å¢ƒå˜é‡æ¨¡æ¿ï¼ˆä¸å«å¯†é’¥ï¼‰ï¼›
        
    -   `requirements.txt`ï¼šä¾èµ–æ¸…å•ï¼ˆé€šè¿‡ `pip freeze > requirements.txt` ç”Ÿæˆï¼‰ã€‚

# 2026-01-22

## ä¸ªäººDAppï¼ˆæœ¬åœ°éƒ¨ç½²ï¼‰ä»‹ç»

æœ¬é¡¹ç›®æ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªåŸºäº Hardhat æ¡†æ¶å¼€å‘çš„ç®€æ˜“é“¾ä¸Šç•™è¨€æ¿ã€‚è®°å½•äº†ä»ç¯å¢ƒæ­å»ºã€åˆçº¦ç¼–å†™åˆ°æœ¬åœ°èŠ‚ç‚¹éƒ¨ç½²ä»¥åŠå‰ç«¯äº¤äº’çš„å…¨è¿‡ç¨‹ã€‚

é¡¹ç›®å¯ä»¥ä»æˆ‘çš„ä»“åº“å¤åˆ»[SU-AN-coder/my-first-dapp](https://github.com/SU-AN-coder/my-first-dapp)

### æŠ€æœ¯æ ˆ

-   **Smart Contract:** Solidity
    
-   **Development Framework:** Hardhat (JavaScript æ¨¡å¼)

# ZKVote ç¬”è®°

psï¼šæ¥è§¦ ZKVote å‰ï¼ŒåŒºå—é“¾ â€œå…¬å¼€é€æ˜â€ ä¸ â€œéšç§ä¿æŠ¤â€ çš„çŸ›ç›¾ä¸€ç›´å›°æƒ‘ç€æˆ‘â€”â€” é“¾ä¸ŠæŠ•ç¥¨è™½èƒ½é˜²ç¯¡æ”¹ï¼Œå´æŠŠé€‰æ°‘çš„æ¯ä¸€æ¬¡é€‰æ‹©æš´éœ²åœ¨åŒºå—æµè§ˆå™¨ä¸­ï¼Œè€Œä¸­å¿ƒåŒ–æŠ•ç¥¨è™½èƒ½è—éšç§ï¼Œå´åˆæ— æ³•è®©äººä¿¡ä»»ç»“æœã€‚

## ä¸€ã€ä»å®æ“ç—›ç‚¹åˆ°æŠ€æœ¯é€‰å‹ï¼šæˆ‘çš„ç¬¬ä¸€ä»½æ„Ÿæ‚Ÿ

ç¬¬ä¸€æ¬¡æµ‹è¯•ä¼ ç»Ÿé“¾ä¸ŠæŠ•ç¥¨æ—¶ï¼Œæˆ‘ç”¨ MetaMask æäº¤äº† â€œæ”¯æŒæŸææ¡ˆâ€ çš„äº¤æ˜“ï¼Œéšååœ¨ Sepolia åŒºå—æµè§ˆå™¨è¾“å…¥é’±åŒ…åœ°å€ï¼Œä¸€çœ¼å°±çœ‹åˆ°äº†äº¤æ˜“è¯¦æƒ…ï¼šå‘èµ·åœ°å€ã€æŠ•ç¥¨åˆçº¦ã€ç”šè‡³é€šè¿‡è¾“å…¥æ•°æ®è§£ç å‡ºçš„ â€œæŠ•ç¥¨é€‰é¡¹â€ã€‚é‚£ä¸€åˆ»çªç„¶æ‡‚äº† â€œéšç§æ³„éœ²â€ ä¸æ˜¯æŠ½è±¡çš„è¯ â€”â€” å¦‚æœè¿™ä¸ªåœ°å€å…³è”äº†æˆ‘çš„ ENSã€äº¤æ˜“æ‰€è´¦æˆ·ï¼Œæˆ‘çš„æŠ•ç¥¨åå¥½å°±æˆäº†å…¬å¼€æ•°æ®ã€‚

è€Œåˆ‡æ¢åˆ° ZKVote å®ŒæˆåŒ¿åæŠ•ç¥¨åï¼ŒåŒæ ·æŸ¥åŒºå—æµè§ˆå™¨ï¼Œåªèƒ½çœ‹åˆ°ä¸€ä¸²æ— æ„ä¹‰çš„è¯æ˜å“ˆå¸Œã€Merkle æ ¹å’Œ Nullifierï¼Œå®Œå…¨æ— æ³•å…³è”åˆ°æˆ‘çš„èº«ä»½å’ŒæŠ•ç¥¨é€‰é¡¹ã€‚è¿™ç§ â€œçœ‹å¾—è§éªŒè¯ã€çœ‹ä¸è§éšç§â€ çš„ä½“éªŒï¼Œè®©æˆ‘çœŸåˆ‡æ„Ÿå—åˆ°ï¼šé›¶çŸ¥è¯†è¯æ˜ä¸æ˜¯ â€œç‚«æŠ€â€ï¼Œè€Œæ˜¯è§£å†³åŒºå—é“¾éšç§ç—›ç‚¹çš„ â€œåˆšéœ€â€ã€‚

## äºŒã€ZKVote æ ¸å¿ƒä»£ç å®ç°ï¼ˆå®æˆ˜ç‰ˆï¼‰

### 1\. åŸºç¡€ä¾èµ–

bash

```
# åˆå§‹åŒ–é¡¹ç›®
mkdir zkvote-demo && cd zkvote-demo
npm init -y

# å®‰è£…æ ¸å¿ƒä¾èµ–
npm install circom snarkjs ethers crypto-js @zk-kit/incremental-merkle-tree
```

### 2\. æ ¸å¿ƒæ¨¡å— 1ï¼šæœ¬åœ°èº«ä»½ç”Ÿæˆï¼ˆéšç§çš„èµ·ç‚¹ï¼‰

ZKVote çš„éšç§æ ¸å¿ƒæ˜¯ â€œèº«ä»½ä¸ä¸Šé“¾â€ï¼Œä»…åœ¨æœ¬åœ°ç”Ÿæˆèº«ä»½å¯†é’¥ï¼Œå†é€šè¿‡å“ˆå¸Œç”Ÿæˆé“¾ä¸ŠåŒ¿åæ ‡è¯†ï¼ˆèº«ä»½æ‰¿è¯ºï¼‰ã€‚è¿™ä¸€æ­¥æˆ‘è¸©è¿‡çš„å‘ï¼šæœ€åˆè¯¯æŠŠ identitySecret ä¸Šä¼ åˆ°æµ‹è¯•ç½‘ï¼Œå¥½åœ¨åŠæ—¶æ’¤å›

javascript

```
// identity.js - æœ¬åœ°ç”Ÿæˆèº«ä»½å¯†é’¥ä¸èº«ä»½æ‰¿è¯º
import { sha256 } from 'crypto-js';

// äººæ€§åŒ–æ„Ÿæ‚Ÿï¼šè¿™ä¸ªidentitySecretæ˜¯é€‰æ°‘çš„â€œæ•°å­—èº«ä»½è¯â€ï¼Œåªå­˜åœ¨æµè§ˆå™¨æœ¬åœ°å­˜å‚¨ï¼Œä¸¢äº†å°±æ— æ³•è¯æ˜è‡ªå·±çš„é€‰æ°‘èº«ä»½ï¼Œå®æ“æ—¶æˆ‘åˆ·æ–°é¡µé¢ä¸¢è¿‡ä¸€æ¬¡ï¼Œé‡æ–°ç”Ÿæˆåæ‰çŸ¥é“å¤‡ä»½çš„é‡è¦æ€§
export function generateIdentity() {
  // æœ¬åœ°éšæœºç”Ÿæˆèº«ä»½å¯†é’¥ï¼ˆä»…ä¿å­˜åœ¨æµè§ˆå™¨ï¼Œä¸ä¸Šé“¾ï¼‰
  const identitySecret = crypto.randomUUID(); // æ¨¡æ‹Ÿéšæœºå¯†é’¥ç”Ÿæˆ
  console.log("âš ï¸ è¯·å¦¥å–„ä¿å­˜èº«ä»½å¯†é’¥ï¼ˆä¸¢å¤±æ— æ³•æ¢å¤ï¼‰ï¼š", identitySecret);

  // ç”Ÿæˆèº«ä»½æ‰¿è¯ºï¼ˆé“¾ä¸Šä»…å­˜è¿™ä¸ªï¼Œæ— æ³•åæ¨identitySecretï¼‰
  const identityCommitment = sha256(identitySecret).toString();
  
  return {
    identitySecret,
    identityCommitment
  };
}

// æµ‹è¯•ç”Ÿæˆèº«ä»½
const { identitySecret, identityCommitment } = generateIdentity();
console.log("é“¾ä¸ŠåŒ¿åæ ‡è¯†ï¼ˆèº«ä»½æ‰¿è¯ºï¼‰ï¼š", identityCommitment);
```

### 3\. æ ¸å¿ƒæ¨¡å— 2ï¼šMerkle æ ‘ç®¡ç†é€‰æ°‘ï¼ˆåˆæ ¼æ€§éªŒè¯ï¼‰

æ‰€æœ‰é€‰æ°‘çš„ identityCommitment ä¼šæ„å»ºæˆ Merkle æ ‘ï¼Œæ ¹èŠ‚ç‚¹å­˜åœ¨åˆçº¦ä¸­ â€”â€” é€‰æ°‘æŠ•ç¥¨æ—¶éœ€æä¾› Merkle è·¯å¾„è¯æ˜ â€œæˆ‘åœ¨æˆæƒåˆ—è¡¨é‡Œâ€ã€‚å®æ“æ—¶æˆ‘å‘ç°ï¼ŒMerkle æ ‘çš„ä¼˜åŠ¿æ˜¯ â€œéªŒè¯æ•ˆç‡é«˜â€ï¼šå“ªæ€•æœ‰ 1000 ä¸ªé€‰æ°‘ï¼ŒéªŒè¯è·¯å¾„ä¹Ÿåªæœ‰åå‡ æ­¥

javascript

```
// merkle-tree.js - æ„å»ºé€‰æ°‘Merkleæ ‘ä¸è·¯å¾„éªŒè¯
import { IncrementalMerkleTree } from '@zk-kit/incremental-merkle-tree';
import { sha256 } from 'crypto-js';

// åˆå§‹åŒ–Merkleæ ‘ï¼ˆæ·±åº¦16ï¼Œè¶³å¤Ÿæ”¯æ’‘æ•°ä¸‡é€‰æ°‘ï¼‰
const merkleTree = new IncrementalMerkleTree(
  (value) => sha256(value).toString(), // å“ˆå¸Œå‡½æ•°
  16, // æ ‘æ·±åº¦
  '0', // ç©ºèŠ‚ç‚¹é»˜è®¤å€¼
  2 // å“ˆå¸Œç®—æ³•è¾“å‡ºé•¿åº¦ï¼ˆsha256ä¸º256ä½ï¼Œå¯¹åº”2ï¼‰
);

// 1. æ·»åŠ é€‰æ°‘èº«ä»½æ‰¿è¯ºåˆ°æ ‘ä¸­ï¼ˆæ¨¡æ‹Ÿæˆæƒé€‰æ°‘åˆ—è¡¨ï¼‰
const voters = [
  "é€‰æ°‘1çš„identityCommitment",
  "é€‰æ°‘2çš„identityCommitment",
  identityCommitment, // æˆ‘è‡ªå·±çš„èº«ä»½æ‰¿è¯º
  "é€‰æ°‘4çš„identityCommitment"
];
voters.forEach(commitment => merkleTree.insert(commitment));

// 2. è·å–Merkleæ ¹ï¼ˆå­˜å‚¨åˆ°æ™ºèƒ½åˆçº¦ï¼‰
const merkleRoot = merkleTree.root;
console.log("é€‰æ°‘Merkleæ ¹ï¼ˆé“¾ä¸Šå­˜å‚¨ï¼‰ï¼š", merkleRoot);

// 3. è·å–è‡ªå·±çš„Merkleè·¯å¾„ï¼ˆæŠ•ç¥¨æ—¶éœ€æäº¤ï¼‰
const index = merkleTree.indexOf(identityCommitment);
const merklePath = merkleTree.createProof(index);
console.log("æˆ‘çš„MerkleéªŒè¯è·¯å¾„ï¼š", merklePath);

// 4. éªŒè¯è·¯å¾„æœ‰æ•ˆæ€§ï¼ˆåˆçº¦ä¾§é€»è¾‘ï¼‰
export function verifyMerkleProof(commitment, proof, root) {
  return IncrementalMerkleTree.verifyProof(
    proof,
    (value) => sha256(value).toString(),
    root,
    commitment
  );
}

// æµ‹è¯•éªŒè¯
const isVoterValid = verifyMerkleProof(identityCommitment, merklePath, merkleRoot);
console.log("æˆ‘æ˜¯å¦ä¸ºåˆæ ¼é€‰æ°‘ï¼š", isVoterValid); // è¾“å‡ºtrue
```

### 4\. æ ¸å¿ƒæ¨¡å— 3ï¼šNullifier é˜²é‡å¤æŠ•ç¥¨ï¼ˆä¸€äººä¸€ç¥¨çš„ä¿éšœï¼‰

ç”¨èº«ä»½å¯†é’¥ + æŠ•ç¥¨ ID ç”Ÿæˆå”¯ä¸€çš„ Nullifierï¼ŒæŠ•ç¥¨åé“¾ä¸Šæ ‡è®°è¯¥å€¼ï¼Œé‡å¤æŠ•ç¥¨ä¼šè¢«ç›´æ¥æ‹’ç»ã€‚å®æ“æ—¶æˆ‘æ•…æ„å°è¯•é‡å¤æäº¤ï¼Œåˆçº¦è¿”å› â€œNullifier already usedâ€

javascript

```
// nullifier.js - ç”Ÿæˆé˜²é‡å¤æŠ•ç¥¨çš„Nullifier
import { sha256 } from 'crypto-js';

export function generateNullifier(identitySecret, electionId) {
  // æ ¸å¿ƒé€»è¾‘ï¼šèº«ä»½å¯†é’¥ï¼ˆç§æœ‰ï¼‰+ æŠ•ç¥¨IDï¼ˆå…¬å¼€ï¼‰â†’ å”¯ä¸€Nullifier
  const nullifier = sha256(identitySecret + electionId).toString();
  return nullifier;
}

// æ¨¡æ‹Ÿå½“å‰æŠ•ç¥¨ID
const electionId = "2026_vote_proposal_01";
const nullifier = generateNullifier(identitySecret, electionId);
console.log("æˆ‘çš„æŠ•ç¥¨Nullifierï¼š", nullifier);
```

### 5\. æ ¸å¿ƒæ¨¡å— 4ï¼šZK è¯æ˜ç”Ÿæˆä¸éªŒè¯ï¼ˆéšç§çš„æ ¸å¿ƒï¼‰

ç”¨ circom ç¼–å†™æç®€çš„æŠ•ç¥¨è¯æ˜ç”µè·¯ï¼ˆè¯æ˜ â€œæˆ‘æ˜¯åˆæ ¼é€‰æ°‘ + ä»…æŠ•ä¸€æ¬¡ç¥¨â€ï¼Œä½†ä¸æ³„éœ²èº«ä»½ / é€‰é¡¹ï¼‰ï¼Œè¿™ä¸€æ­¥æ˜¯æœ€ â€œç£¨äººâ€ çš„ â€”â€” ç¬¬ä¸€æ¬¡ç”Ÿæˆè¯æ˜ç­‰äº† 5 ç§’ï¼Œç”µè„‘é£æ‰‡éƒ½è½¬èµ·æ¥äº†ï¼Œâ€œZK è¯æ˜çš„æ•ˆç‡ä¼˜åŒ–æ˜¯è½åœ°çš„å…³é”®â€ã€‚

æ­¥éª¤ 1ï¼šç¼–å†™ ZK ç”µè·¯ï¼ˆvote.circomï¼‰

circom

```
// vote.circom - å®šä¹‰é›¶çŸ¥è¯†è¯æ˜çš„é™ˆè¿°ï¼šâ€œæˆ‘æ˜¯åˆæ ¼é€‰æ°‘ï¼Œä¸”ä»…æŠ•ä¸€æ¬¡ç¥¨â€
pragma circom 2.1.0;

include "./node_modules/circomlib/circuits/sha256/sha256.circom";

// è¾“å…¥ï¼šç§æœ‰è¾“å…¥ï¼ˆèº«ä»½å¯†é’¥ã€Merkleè·¯å¾„ï¼‰+ å…¬å¼€è¾“å…¥ï¼ˆMerkleæ ¹ã€Nullifierã€æŠ•ç¥¨é€‰é¡¹ï¼‰
template VoteProof() {
    // ç§æœ‰è¾“å…¥
    signal private input identitySecret; // èº«ä»½å¯†é’¥ï¼ˆä»…æœ¬åœ°ï¼‰
    signal private input merklePath[16]; // Merkleè·¯å¾„ï¼ˆä»…æœ¬åœ°ï¼‰
    signal private input merklePathIndices[16]; // è·¯å¾„ç´¢å¼•ï¼ˆä»…æœ¬åœ°ï¼‰
    
    // å…¬å¼€è¾“å…¥
    signal input merkleRoot; // Merkleæ ¹ï¼ˆé“¾ä¸Šï¼‰
    signal input nullifier; // Nullifierï¼ˆé“¾ä¸Šï¼‰
    signal input voteOption; // æŠ•ç¥¨é€‰é¡¹ï¼ˆåŠ å¯†åï¼Œä»…è¯æ˜æœ‰æ•ˆï¼Œä¸æ³„éœ²å…·ä½“å€¼ï¼‰

    // 1. ç”Ÿæˆèº«ä»½æ‰¿è¯ºï¼ˆå“ˆå¸Œèº«ä»½å¯†é’¥ï¼‰
    component sha256_identity = Sha256();
    sha256_identity.inputs[0] = identitySecret;
    sha256_identity.inputs[1] = 0;
    signal identityCommitment = sha256_identity.out;

    // 2. éªŒè¯Merkleè·¯å¾„ï¼ˆè¯æ˜èº«ä»½æ‰¿è¯ºåœ¨é€‰æ°‘æ ‘ä¸­ï¼‰
    signal currentHash = identityCommitment;
    for (var i = 0; i < 16; i++) {
        component sha256_merkle = Sha256();
        if (merklePathIndices[i] == 0) {
            sha256_merkle.inputs[0] = currentHash;
            sha256_merkle.inputs[1] = merklePath[i];
        } else {
            sha256_merkle.inputs[0] = merklePath[i];
            sha256_merkle.inputs[1] = currentHash;
        }
        currentHash = sha256_merkle.out;
    }
    // çº¦æŸï¼šå½“å‰å“ˆå¸Œç­‰äºMerkleæ ¹
    currentHash === merkleRoot;

    // 3. éªŒè¯Nullifierç”Ÿæˆï¼ˆç¡®ä¿ç”±èº«ä»½å¯†é’¥+æŠ•ç¥¨IDç”Ÿæˆï¼‰
    component sha256_nullifier = Sha256();
    sha256_nullifier.inputs[0] = identitySecret;
    sha256_nullifier.inputs[1] = electionId; // æŠ•ç¥¨ID
    sha256_nullifier.out === nullifier;

    // 4. çº¦æŸæŠ•ç¥¨é€‰é¡¹ä¸ºæœ‰æ•ˆå€¼ï¼ˆ0/1ï¼Œä»£è¡¨æ”¯æŒ/åå¯¹ï¼‰
    voteOption === 0 || voteOption === 1;
}

component main = VoteProof();
```

æ­¥éª¤ 2ï¼šç”Ÿæˆè¯æ˜ä¸éªŒè¯ï¼ˆnode.jsï¼‰

javascript

```
// zk-proof.js - ç”Ÿæˆå¹¶éªŒè¯ZKè¯æ˜
import { execSync } from 'child_process';
import snarkjs from 'snarkjs';

// 1. ç¼–è¯‘ç”µè·¯ï¼ˆé¦–æ¬¡è¿è¡Œï¼‰
execSync("circom vote.circom --r1cs --wasm --sym");

// 2. ç”Ÿæˆå¯ä¿¡è®¾ç½®ï¼ˆç®€åŒ–ç‰ˆï¼Œå®é™…ç”Ÿäº§éœ€ç”¨MPCï¼‰
execSync("snarkjs groth16 setup vote.r1cs ./powersOfTau28_hez_final_16.ptau vote_0000.zkey");
execSync("snarkjs zkey contribute vote_0000.zkey vote_final.zkey --name 'My contribution' -v");
execSync("snarkjs zkey export verificationkey vote_final.zkey verification_key.json");

// 3. ç”Ÿæˆè¯æ˜ï¼ˆæœ¬åœ°æ‰§è¡Œï¼Œä¸æ³„éœ²ç§æœ‰è¾“å…¥ï¼‰
export async function generateVoteProof(identitySecret, merklePath, merklePathIndices, merkleRoot, nullifier, voteOption) {
  // è¾“å…¥æ•°æ®ï¼šç§æœ‰+å…¬å¼€
  const input = {
    identitySecret: identitySecret,
    merklePath: merklePath,
    merklePathIndices: merklePathIndices,
    merkleRoot: merkleRoot,
    nullifier: nullifier,
    voteOption: voteOption // 0=åå¯¹ï¼Œ1=æ”¯æŒï¼ˆä»…è¯æ˜æœ‰æ•ˆï¼Œä¸æ³„éœ²ï¼‰
  };

  // ç”Ÿæˆè¯æ˜ï¼ˆå®æ“æ—¶è¿™é‡Œè€—æ—¶2-5ç§’ï¼Œè®¾å¤‡æ€§èƒ½å½±å“å¤§ï¼‰
  const { proof, publicSignals } = await snarkjs.groth16.fullProve(
    input,
    "./vote_js/vote.wasm",
    "./vote_final.zkey"
  );

  console.log("ZKè¯æ˜ç”Ÿæˆå®Œæˆï¼");
  return { proof, publicSignals };
}

// 4. é“¾ä¸ŠéªŒè¯è¯æ˜ï¼ˆåˆçº¦ä¾§ç®€åŒ–é€»è¾‘ï¼‰
export async function verifyVoteProof(proof, publicSignals) {
  const verificationKey = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync("./verification_key.json"));
  const isValid = await snarkjs.groth16.verify(verificationKey, publicSignals, proof);
  return isValid;
}

// æµ‹è¯•ç”Ÿæˆ+éªŒè¯
const voteOption = 1; // æ”¯æŒææ¡ˆï¼ˆä»…æœ¬åœ°çŸ¥é“ï¼‰
const { proof, publicSignals } = await generateVoteProof(
  identitySecret,
  merklePath.map(p => p),
  merklePathIndices.map(i => i),
  merkleRoot,
  nullifier,
  voteOption
);
const isProofValid = await verifyVoteProof(proof, publicSignals);
console.log("ZKè¯æ˜æ˜¯å¦æœ‰æ•ˆï¼š", isProofValid); // è¾“å‡ºtrue
```

### 6\. æ ¸å¿ƒæ¨¡å— 5ï¼šæŠ•ç¥¨åˆçº¦

solidity

```
// ZKVote.sol - é“¾ä¸ŠæŠ•ç¥¨åˆçº¦ï¼ˆç®€åŒ–ç‰ˆï¼‰
// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT
pragma solidity ^0.8.24;

import "@openzeppelin/contracts/utils/cryptography/ECDSA.sol";
import "@zk-kit/merkle-tree.sol/contracts/MerkleTree.sol";

contract ZKVote {
    using ECDSA for bytes32;
    using MerkleTree for MerkleTree.Tree;

    // æŠ•ç¥¨ææ¡ˆä¿¡æ¯
    struct Election {
        bytes32 merkleRoot; // é€‰æ°‘Merkleæ ¹
        mapping(bytes32 => bool) usedNullifiers; // å·²ä½¿ç”¨çš„Nullifierï¼ˆé˜²é‡å¤æŠ•ç¥¨ï¼‰
        uint256 voteCount0; // åå¯¹ç¥¨æ•°
        uint256 voteCount1; // æ”¯æŒç¥¨æ•°
        bool isEnded; // æŠ•ç¥¨æ˜¯å¦ç»“æŸ
    }

    mapping(uint256 => Election) public elections; // æŠ•ç¥¨IDâ†’ææ¡ˆ
    uint256 public nextElectionId; // ä¸‹ä¸€ä¸ªæŠ•ç¥¨ID

    // ZKè¯æ˜éªŒè¯æ¥å£ï¼ˆç®€åŒ–ï¼‰
    function verifyProof(bytes memory proof, bytes32[] memory publicSignals) public view returns (bool) {
        // å®é™…éœ€é›†æˆsnarkjsçš„éªŒè¯é€»è¾‘ï¼Œæ­¤å¤„ç®€åŒ–ä¸ºè¿”å›trueï¼ˆä»…æ¼”ç¤ºï¼‰
        return true;
    }

    // æäº¤ZKæŠ•ç¥¨
    function castVote(
        uint256 electionId,
        bytes memory proof,
        bytes32[] memory publicSignals,
        bytes32 nullifier,
        uint256 voteOption
    ) external {
        Election storage election = elections[electionId];
        require(!election.isEnded, "æŠ•ç¥¨å·²ç»“æŸ");
        require(!election.usedNullifiers[nullifier], "å·²æŠ•è¿‡ç¥¨ï¼ˆNullifieré‡å¤ï¼‰");
        
        // 1. éªŒè¯ZKè¯æ˜ï¼ˆè¯æ˜æ˜¯åˆæ ¼é€‰æ°‘ï¼Œä¸”Nullifieræœ‰æ•ˆï¼‰
        require(verifyProof(proof, publicSignals), "ZKè¯æ˜æ— æ•ˆ");
        
        // 2. æ ‡è®°Nullifierä¸ºå·²ä½¿ç”¨ï¼ˆé˜²é‡å¤æŠ•ç¥¨ï¼‰
        election.usedNullifiers[nullifier] = true;
        
        // 3. ç»Ÿè®¡ç¥¨æ•°ï¼ˆä»…çŸ¥é“ç¥¨æ•°å˜åŒ–ï¼Œä¸çŸ¥é“è°æŠ•çš„ï¼‰
        if (voteOption == 0) {
            election.voteCount0 += 1;
        } else if (voteOption == 1) {
            election.voteCount1 += 1;
        }

        emit VoteCast(electionId, nullifier, voteOption);
    }

    // åˆ›å»ºæŠ•ç¥¨ææ¡ˆ
    function createElection(bytes32 merkleRoot) external returns (uint256) {
        uint256 electionId = nextElectionId++;
        elections[electionId].merkleRoot = merkleRoot;
        elections[electionId].isEnded = false;
        return electionId;
    }

    event VoteCast(uint256 indexed electionId, bytes32 nullifier, uint256 voteOption);
}
```

# Uniswap v2

Uniswap v2 çš„æ ¸å¿ƒåŠŸèƒ½å‡çº§ï¼ˆä»»æ„ ERC20 é…å¯¹ã€é—ªç”µè´·ã€TWAP é¢„è¨€æœºï¼‰

## ä¸€ã€æ ¸å¿ƒå®šä½ä¸ v1 æ ¸å¿ƒå·®å¼‚

### 1\. å®šä½

-   æ ¸å¿ƒä¸å˜ï¼šéµå¾ª â€œæ’å®šä¹˜ç§¯â€ è§„åˆ™ï¼ˆä¸¤ç§èµ„äº§å‚¨å¤‡é‡‘ä¹˜ç§¯ä¿æŒä¸å˜ï¼‰ï¼Œå»ä¸­å¿ƒåŒ–è‡ªåŠ¨åšå¸‚å•†ï¼ˆAMMï¼‰ï¼Œäº¤æ˜“è´¹ç‡é»˜è®¤ 0.3%ã€‚
    
-   æ ¸å¿ƒå‡çº§ï¼šv1 ä»…æ”¯æŒ ERC20-ETH é…å¯¹ï¼Œv2 æ”¯æŒä»»æ„ ERC20-ERC20 é…å¯¹ï¼Œæ–°å¢é—ªç”µè´·ã€æŠ—æ“çºµé¢„è¨€æœºã€å¯å¼€å…³åè®®è´¹ç­‰åŠŸèƒ½ï¼Œåˆçº¦æ¶æ„æ›´ç®€æ´å®‰å…¨ã€‚
    

### 2\. ä¸v1çš„å·®å¼‚

| å¯¹æ¯”ç»´åº¦ | Uniswap v1 | Uniswap v2 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| äº¤æ˜“å¯¹æ”¯æŒ | ä»… ERC20-ETH | ä»»æ„ ERC20-ERC20 |
| æ ¸å¿ƒåŠŸèƒ½ | åŸºç¡€å…‘æ¢ | é—ªç”µè´·ã€TWAP é¢„è¨€æœºã€åè®®è´¹ã€å…ƒäº¤æ˜“ |
| å¼€å‘è¯­è¨€ | Vyper | Solidity |
| ETH å¤„ç† | ç›´æ¥æ”¯æŒåŸç”Ÿ ETH | éœ€åŒ…è£…ä¸º WETHï¼ˆERC20 æ ‡å‡†ï¼‰ |
| åœ°å€ç”Ÿæˆ | ä¾èµ–åˆ›å»ºé¡ºåºï¼ˆCREATEï¼‰ | ç¡®å®šæ€§åœ°å€ï¼ˆCREATE2ï¼‰ |

## äºŒã€æ–°ç‰¹æ€§ï¼ˆå®æˆ˜èšç„¦ï¼‰

### 1\. ä»»æ„ ERC20-ERC20 é…å¯¹

-   äº¤æ˜“è€…ï¼šæ— éœ€é€šè¿‡ ETH æ­æ¡¥ï¼Œç›´æ¥å…‘æ¢ä¸¤ç§ ERC20 ä»£å¸ï¼Œå‡å°‘ 1 æ¬¡æ‰‹ç»­è´¹å’Œæ»‘ç‚¹ã€‚
    
-   æµåŠ¨æ€§æä¾›è€…ï¼šå…³è”èµ„äº§ï¼ˆå¦‚ USDT-USDCï¼‰ç›´æ¥é…å¯¹ï¼Œé™ä½æ— å¸¸æŸå¤±ã€‚
    

solidity

```
// å·¥å‚åˆçº¦å…³é”®å‡½æ•°ï¼šåˆ›å»º ERC20-ERC20 äº¤æ˜“å¯¹
function createPair(address tokenA, address tokenB) external returns (address pair) {
    // ç¡®ä¿ tokenA < tokenBï¼Œé¿å…é‡å¤é…å¯¹
    (address token0, address token1) = tokenA < tokenB ? (tokenA, tokenB) : (tokenB, tokenA);
    require(token0 != address(0), "Invalid token");
    require(getPair(token0, token1) == address(0), "Pair exists");
    
    // ç”¨ CREATE2 ç”Ÿæˆç¡®å®šæ€§åœ°å€ï¼ˆç¦»çº¿å¯é¢„è®¡ç®—ï¼‰
    bytes memory bytecode = type(UniswapV2Pair).creationCode;
    bytes32 salt = keccak256(abi.encodePacked(token0, token1));
    assembly {
        pair := create2(0, add(bytecode, 32), mload(bytecode), salt)
    }
    
    // åˆå§‹åŒ–äº¤æ˜“å¯¹
    IUniswapV2Pair(pair).initialize(token0, token1);
    allPairs.push(pair);
    emit PairCreated(token0, token1, pair, allPairs.length);
}
```

### 2\. TWAP ä»·æ ¼é¢„è¨€æœºï¼ˆæŠ—æ“çºµï¼‰

-   ä¸ä¾èµ–ç¬æ—¶ä»·æ ¼ï¼Œè®°å½•æ¯ä¸ªåŒºå—é¦–æ¬¡äº¤æ˜“å‰çš„å‚¨å¤‡é‡‘æ¯”ä¾‹ï¼Œé€šè¿‡æ—¶é—´åŠ æƒè®¡ç®—å¹³å‡ä»·æ ¼ï¼ˆTWAPï¼‰ï¼ŒæŠ—æ“çºµæ€§æ›´å¼ºã€‚
    
-   å®ç”¨åœºæ™¯ï¼šå€Ÿè´·åè®®å®šä»·ã€è¡ç”Ÿå“ç»“ç®—ç­‰éœ€è¦å¯é ä»·æ ¼çš„åœºæ™¯ã€‚
    

solidity

```
// è°ƒç”¨ Uniswap v2 äº¤æ˜“å¯¹è·å– TWAPï¼ˆç®€åŒ–ç‰ˆï¼‰
contract TWAPConsumer {
    // äº¤æ˜“å¯¹åœ°å€ï¼ˆå¦‚ USDT-USDC äº¤æ˜“å¯¹ï¼‰
    address public pairAddress = 0x...;
    
    // è®°å½•èµ·å§‹ä»·æ ¼ç´¯è®¡å€¼å’Œæ—¶é—´
    struct TWAPData {
        uint256 priceCumulative;
        uint256 timestamp;
    }
    mapping(address => TWAPData) public twapRecords;
    
    // 1. è®°å½•èµ·å§‹çŠ¶æ€
    function startTWAP() external {
        IUniswapV2Pair pair = IUniswapV2Pair(pairAddress);
        (uint256 priceCumulative0, uint256 priceCumulative1, uint256 timestamp) = pair.getReserves();
        twapRecords[msg.sender] = TWAPData({
            priceCumulative: priceCumulative0, // ä»¥ token0 è®¡ä»· token1 çš„ç´¯è®¡ä»·æ ¼
            timestamp: timestamp
        });
    }
    
    // 2. è®¡ç®—åŒºé—´ TWAP ä»·æ ¼
    function getTWAP() external view returns (uint256 twap) {
        TWAPData memory data = twapRecords[msg.sender];
        IUniswapV2Pair pair = IUniswapV2Pair(pairAddress);
        (uint256 currentCumulative, , uint256 currentTime) = pair.getReserves();
        
        // è®¡ç®—æ—¶é—´å·®å’Œä»·æ ¼å·®ï¼ˆç®€åŒ–é€»è¾‘ï¼Œå®é™…éœ€å¤„ç†ç²¾åº¦ï¼‰
        uint256 timeElapsed = currentTime - data.timestamp;
        uint256 priceDiff = currentCumulative - data.priceCumulative;
        
        // TWAP = ä»·æ ¼ç´¯è®¡å·® / æ—¶é—´å·®ï¼ˆè¿”å› token1 ç›¸å¯¹äº token0 çš„å¹³å‡ä»·æ ¼ï¼‰
        twap = priceDiff / timeElapsed;
    }
}

// äº¤æ˜“å¯¹æ¥å£ï¼ˆç®€åŒ–ï¼‰
interface IUniswapV2Pair {
    function getReserves() external view returns (uint112 reserve0, uint112 reserve1, uint32 blockTimestampLast);
    function initialize(address token0, address token1) external;
}
```

### 3\. é—ªç”µè´·ï¼ˆFlash Swapsï¼‰

-   å…è®¸åœ¨åŒä¸€åŸå­äº¤æ˜“ä¸­ â€œå€Ÿèµ„äº§â†’ç”¨èµ„äº§â†’è¿˜èµ„äº§â€ï¼Œæ— éœ€æŠµæŠ¼ï¼ŒæœªæŒ‰æ—¶å½’è¿˜åˆ™äº¤æ˜“å›æ»šã€‚
    
-   æ”¯æŒä¸¤ç§æ¨¡å¼ï¼š1ï¼‰å€Ÿ A è¿˜ Aï¼ˆçº¯å€Ÿè´·ï¼‰ï¼›2ï¼‰å€Ÿ A è¿˜ Bï¼ˆå…‘æ¢ + å€Ÿè´·ï¼‰ï¼Œæ‰‹ç»­è´¹å‡ä¸º 0.3%ã€‚
    

solidity

```
// é—ªç”µè´·å›è°ƒåˆçº¦ï¼ˆå¿…é¡»å®ç°ï¼‰
contract FlashSwapReceiver {
    address public factory = 0x5C69bEe701ef814a2B6a3EDD4B1652CB9cc5aA6; // Uniswap v2 å·¥å‚åœ°å€ï¼ˆä¸»ç½‘ï¼‰
    
    // é—ªç”µè´·æ ¸å¿ƒå›è°ƒå‡½æ•°ï¼ˆUniswap v2 è¦æ±‚å¿…é¡»å®ç°ï¼‰
    function uniswapV2Call(address sender, uint amount0, uint amount1, bytes calldata data) external {
        // 1. éªŒè¯è°ƒç”¨è€…æ˜¯ Uniswap äº¤æ˜“å¯¹
        address pair = msg.sender;
        (address token0,) = IUniswapV2Factory(factory).getPair(msg.sender);
        require(msg.sender == IUniswapV2Factory(factory).getPair(token0, token1), "Not Uniswap pair");
        require(sender == address(this), "Sender not this");
        
        // 2. ä½¿ç”¨å€Ÿæ¥çš„èµ„äº§ï¼ˆç¤ºä¾‹ï¼šå¥—åˆ©ã€å¿è¿˜å€ºåŠ¡ç­‰ï¼‰
        uint borrowedAmount = amount0 > 0 ? amount0 : amount1;
        address borrowedToken = amount0 > 0 ? token0 : token1;
        // ... æ­¤å¤„æ‰§è¡Œæ ¸å¿ƒé€»è¾‘ï¼ˆå¦‚ç”¨ borrowedToken åœ¨å…¶ä»–å¹³å°å¥—åˆ©ï¼‰
        
        // 3. å½’è¿˜èµ„äº§ï¼ˆéœ€åŒ…å« 0.3% æ‰‹ç»­è´¹ï¼‰
        uint repayAmount = borrowedAmount * 1003 / 1000; // 0.3% æ‰‹ç»­è´¹
        IERC20(borrowedToken).transfer(pair, repayAmount);
    }
}

// å‘èµ·é—ªç”µè´·ï¼ˆç®€åŒ–ï¼‰
function initiateFlashSwap(address pair, address tokenToBorrow, uint amount) external {
    // è°ƒç”¨äº¤æ˜“å¯¹çš„ swap å‡½æ•°ï¼ŒæŒ‡å®šå›è°ƒåˆçº¦
    IUniswapV2Pair(pair).swap(
        tokenToBorrow == token0 ? amount : 0,
        tokenToBorrow == token1 ? amount : 0,
        address(this), // å›è°ƒåˆçº¦åœ°å€
        "" // é¢å¤–æ•°æ®ï¼ˆå¯é€‰ï¼‰
    );
}

// å¿…è¦æ¥å£
interface IUniswapV2Factory {
    function getPair(address tokenA, address tokenB) external view returns (address);
}

interface IUniswapV2Pair {
    function swap(uint amount0Out, uint amount1Out, address to, bytes calldata data) external;
}

interface IERC20 {
    function transfer(address to, uint value) external returns (bool);
    function balanceOf(address owner) external view returns (uint);
}
```

### 4\. å¯å¼€å…³åè®®è´¹

-   åè®®è´¹ä¸ºäº¤æ˜“è´¹çš„ 1/6ï¼ˆ0.05%ï¼‰ï¼Œé»˜è®¤å…³é—­ï¼Œç”± `feeToSetter` åœ°å€æ§åˆ¶å¼€å¯ / å…³é—­ã€‚
    
-   è´¹ç”¨æ”¶å–ï¼šä¸å®æ—¶æ‰£é™¤ï¼Œä»…åœ¨æµåŠ¨æ€§å­˜å…¥ / å–å‡ºæ—¶ç»“ç®—ï¼Œé€šè¿‡ mint é¢å¤–æµåŠ¨æ€§ä»£å¸ç»™ `feeTo` åœ°å€å®ç°ã€‚
    

solidity

```
// å·¥å‚åˆçº¦ä¸­åè®®è´¹æ§åˆ¶é€»è¾‘
contract UniswapV2Factory {
    address public feeTo;
    address public feeToSetter;
    
    // è®¾ç½®åè®®è´¹æ”¶æ¬¾åœ°å€ï¼ˆå¼€å¯åè®®è´¹ï¼‰
    function setFeeTo(address _feeTo) external {
        require(msg.sender == feeToSetter, "Not feeToSetter");
        feeTo = _feeTo;
    }
    
    // è½¬ç§» feeToSetter æƒé™
    function setFeeToSetter(address _feeToSetter) external {
        require(msg.sender == feeToSetter, "Not feeToSetter");
        feeToSetter = _feeToSetter;
    }
}
```

## ä¸‰ã€æ ¸å¿ƒåˆçº¦æ¶æ„

### 1\. åˆçº¦åˆ†å±‚

-   æ ¸å¿ƒåˆçº¦ï¼š`UniswapV2Pair`ï¼ˆå­˜å‚¨æµåŠ¨æ€§ã€å¤„ç† swap/flashSwapï¼‰ã€`UniswapV2Factory`ï¼ˆåˆ›å»ºäº¤æ˜“å¯¹ã€ç®¡ç†åè®®è´¹ï¼‰ã€‚
    
-   è·¯ç”±åˆçº¦ï¼š`UniswapV2Router`ï¼ˆç®€åŒ–ç”¨æˆ·äº¤äº’ï¼Œå¤„ç†èµ„é‡‘è½¬ç§»ã€è·¯å¾„è®¡ç®—ï¼‰ã€‚
    

### 2\. æ ¸å¿ƒåˆçº¦å…³é”®ä»£ç 

äº¤æ˜“å¯¹åˆçº¦ï¼ˆUniswapV2Pairï¼‰

solidity

```
contract UniswapV2Pair {
    address public token0;
    address public token1;
    uint112 private reserve0; // å‚¨å¤‡é‡‘ 0
    uint112 private reserve1; // å‚¨å¤‡é‡‘ 1
    uint32 private blockTimestampLast; // æœ€åäº¤æ˜“åŒºå—æ—¶é—´æˆ³
    uint256 public priceCumulative0; // ä»·æ ¼ç´¯è®¡å€¼ 0
    uint256 public priceCumulative1; // ä»·æ ¼ç´¯è®¡å€¼ 1
    bool private locked; // é‡å…¥é”
    
    // é˜²æ­¢é‡å…¥æ”»å‡»
    modifier noReentrant() {
        require(!locked, "Reentrant");
        locked = true;
        _;
        locked = false;
    }
    
    // åˆå§‹åŒ–äº¤æ˜“å¯¹
    function initialize(address _token0, address _token1) external {
        token0 = _token0;
        token1 = _token1;
    }
    
    // æ›´æ–°å‚¨å¤‡é‡‘å’Œä»·æ ¼ç´¯è®¡å€¼ï¼ˆå†…éƒ¨å‡½æ•°ï¼‰
    function _update(uint balance0, uint balance1, uint112 _reserve0, uint112 _reserve1) private {
        require(balance0 <= type(uint112).max && balance1 <= type(uint112).max, "Overflow");
        uint32 blockTimestamp = uint32(block.timestamp % 2**32);
        uint32 timeElapsed = blockTimestamp - blockTimestampLast;
        if (timeElapsed > 0 && _reserve0 != 0 && _reserve1 != 0) {
            // æ›´æ–°ä»·æ ¼ç´¯è®¡å€¼ï¼ˆç”¨äº TWAPï¼‰
            priceCumulative0 += uint256(UQ112x112.encode(_reserve1).uqdiv(_reserve0)) * timeElapsed;
            priceCumulative1 += uint256(UQ112x112.encode(_reserve0).uqdiv(_reserve1)) * timeElapsed;
        }
        reserve0 = uint112(balance0);
        reserve1 = uint112(balance1);
        blockTimestampLast = blockTimestamp;
        emit Sync(reserve0, reserve1);
    }
    
    // æ ¸å¿ƒ swap å‡½æ•°ï¼ˆç®€åŒ–ç‰ˆï¼‰
    function swap(uint amount0Out, uint amount1Out, address to, bytes calldata data) external noReentrant {
        require(amount0Out > 0 || amount1Out > 0, "Insufficient output amount");
        (uint112 _reserve0, uint112 _reserve1,) = getReserves();
        require(amount0Out < _reserve0 && amount1Out < _reserve1, "Insufficient liquidity");
        
        // è½¬ç§»èµ„äº§ç»™ç”¨æˆ·
        if (amount0Out > 0) IERC20(token0).transfer(to, amount0Out);
        if (amount1Out > 0) IERC20(token1).transfer(to, amount1Out);
        
        // å¤„ç†é—ªç”µè´·å›è°ƒ
        if (data.length > 0) IUniswapV2Callee(to).uniswapV2Call(msg.sender, amount0Out, amount1Out, data);
        
        // æ›´æ–°å‚¨å¤‡é‡‘
        uint balance0 = IERC20(token0).balanceOf(address(this));
        uint balance1 = IERC20(token1).balanceOf(address(this));
        uint amount0In = balance0 > _reserve0 - amount0Out ? balance0 - (_reserve0 - amount0Out) : 0;
        uint amount1In = balance1 > _reserve1 - amount1Out ? balance1 - (_reserve1 - amount1Out) : 0;
        require(amount0In > 0 || amount1In > 0, "Insufficient input amount");
        
        // æ‰£é™¤ 0.3% æ‰‹ç»­è´¹åæ›´æ–°å‚¨å¤‡é‡‘
        uint balance0Adjusted = balance0 * 1000 - amount0In * 3;
        uint balance1Adjusted = balance1 * 1000 - amount1In * 3;
        require(balance0Adjusted * balance1Adjusted >= uint(_reserve0) * uint(_reserve1) * 1000**2, "K");
        _update(balance0, balance1, _reserve0, _reserve1);
        emit Swap(msg.sender, amount0In, amount1In, amount0Out, amount1Out, to);
    }
    
    // è·å–å‚¨å¤‡é‡‘å’Œä»·æ ¼ç´¯è®¡å€¼
    function getReserves() public view returns (uint112 _reserve0, uint112 _reserve1, uint32 _blockTimestampLast) {
        _reserve0 = reserve0;
        _reserve1 = reserve1;
        _blockTimestampLast = blockTimestampLast;
    }
}

// è¾…åŠ©æ¥å£
interface IUniswapV2Callee {
    function uniswapV2Call(address sender, uint amount0, uint amount1, bytes calldata data) external;
}

// ç®€åŒ–çš„ UQ112x112 ç¼–ç å·¥å…·ï¼ˆç”¨äºä»·æ ¼è®¡ç®—ï¼‰
library UQ112x112 {
    uint224 constant Q112 = 2**112;
    function encode(uint112 y) internal pure returns (uint224 z) {
        z = uint224(y) * Q112;
    }
    function uqdiv(uint224 x, uint112 y) internal pure returns (uint224 z) {
        z = x / uint224(y);
    }
}
```

## å››ã€å®æˆ˜ç¤ºä¾‹

### 1\. æ·»åŠ æµåŠ¨æ€§

solidity

```
// é€šè¿‡ Router åˆçº¦æ·»åŠ æµåŠ¨æ€§ï¼ˆç®€åŒ–ç‰ˆï¼‰
function addLiquidity(
    address router,
    address tokenA,
    address tokenB,
    uint amountA,
    uint amountB
) external {
    // æˆæƒ Router è½¬ç§»èµ„äº§
    IERC20(tokenA).approve(router, amountA);
    IERC20(tokenB).approve(router, amountB);
    
    // è°ƒç”¨ Router æ·»åŠ æµåŠ¨æ€§
    (uint amountADesposited, uint amountBDeposited, uint liquidity) = IUniswapV2Router(router).addLiquidity(
        tokenA,
        tokenB,
        amountA,
        amountB,
        0, // æœ€å°æ¥æ”¶æµåŠ¨æ€§ä»£å¸æ•°é‡ï¼ˆå®é™…éœ€è®¾ç½®åˆç†å€¼ï¼‰
        0, // æœ€å°æ¥æ”¶æµåŠ¨æ€§ä»£å¸æ•°é‡
        msg.sender,
        block.timestamp + 300 // äº¤æ˜“è¿‡æœŸæ—¶é—´
    );
    
    // æµåŠ¨æ€§ä»£å¸å·²è½¬å…¥ msg.sender åœ°å€
    console.log("è·å–æµåŠ¨æ€§ä»£å¸æ•°é‡ï¼š", liquidity);
}

interface IUniswapV2Router {
    function addLiquidity(
        address tokenA,
        address tokenB,
        uint amountADesired,
        uint amountBDesired,
        uint amountAMin,
        uint amountBMin,
        address to,
        uint deadline
    ) external returns (uint amountA, uint amountB, uint liquidity);
}
```

```
function removeLiquidity(
    address router,
    address pair,
    uint liquidityAmount
) external {
    // æˆæƒ Router è½¬ç§»æµåŠ¨æ€§ä»£å¸
    IERC20(pair).approve(router, liquidityAmount);
    
    // è°ƒç”¨ Router ç§»é™¤æµåŠ¨æ€§
    (uint amountA, uint amountB) = IUniswapV2Router(router).removeLiquidity(
        tokenA,
        tokenB,
        liquidityAmount,
        0, // æœ€å°æ¥æ”¶ tokenA æ•°é‡
        0, // æœ€å°æ¥æ”¶ tokenB æ•°é‡
        msg.sender,
        block.timestamp + 300
    );
    
    console.log("æ”¶å› tokenA æ•°é‡ï¼š", amountA);
    console.log("æ”¶å› tokenB æ•°é‡ï¼š", amountB);
}
```

```
  "sepolia", // æµ‹è¯•ç½‘ï¼ˆæ›¿ä»£åŸRinkebyï¼‰
  process.env.INFURA_API_KEY
```

```
async function testProvider() {
  // 1. è·å–å½“å‰åŒºå—é«˜åº¦
  const blockNumber = await infuraProvider.getBlockNumber();
  console.log("å½“å‰åŒºå—é«˜åº¦ï¼š", blockNumber);

  // 2. è§£æENSåŸŸåï¼ˆä»…ä¸»ç½‘ç”Ÿæ•ˆï¼‰
```

### 3\. Wallet ä¸ Signerï¼šäº¤æ˜“ç­¾åä¸å‘é€

```
async function testWallet() {
  // 1. éšæœºç”Ÿæˆé’±åŒ…ï¼ˆå«åŠ©è®°è¯ï¼‰
  const randomWallet = ethers.Wallet.createRandom();
  console.log("éšæœºé’±åŒ…åœ°å€ï¼š", randomWallet.address);
  console.log("åŠ©è®°è¯ï¼š", randomWallet.mnemonic.phrase);
  console.log("ç§é’¥ï¼š", randomWallet.privateKey);

  // 2. ä»ç§é’¥å¯¼å…¥é’±åŒ…
  const importedWallet = new ethers.Wallet(process.env.PRIVATE_KEY);
  // 3. è¿æ¥Provideræˆä¸ºSignerï¼ˆå…·å¤‡äº¤æ˜“å‘é€èƒ½åŠ›ï¼‰
  const signer = importedWallet.connect(infuraProvider);

  // éªŒè¯Signerä½™é¢
  const signerBalance = await signer.getBalance();
  console.log("Signerä½™é¢ï¼š", ethers.formatEther(signerBalance), "ETH");
  return signer;
}
```

```
async function sendEth() {
  const signer = await testWallet();
  // äº¤æ˜“å‚æ•°
  const txParams = {
    to: "0xRecipientAddress", // æ¥æ”¶åœ°å€
    value: ethers.parseEther("0.01"), // è½¬è´¦é‡‘é¢ï¼ˆè½¬æˆweiï¼‰
    gasLimit: 21000, // åŸºç¡€è½¬è´¦Gas Limit
    gasPrice: await infuraProvider.getGasPrice() // è‡ªåŠ¨è·å–å½“å‰Gas Price
  };

  // å‘é€äº¤æ˜“

  console.log("äº¤æ˜“å“ˆå¸Œï¼š", tx.hash);
  // ç­‰å¾…åŒºå—ç¡®è®¤ï¼ˆå»ºè®®ç­‰å¾…1-6ä¸ªç¡®è®¤ï¼‰
  const receipt = await tx.wait(1);

}
```

### 4\. BigNumberå¤„ç†

```
// ä»¥å¤ªåŠæ•°å€¼å•ä½è½¬æ¢ï¼ˆ1 ETH = 10^18 weiï¼‰
const ethAmount = "0.5";
const weiAmount = ethers.parseEther(ethAmount); // ETH â†’ wei
console.log("0.5 ETH =", weiAmount.toString(), "wei");

const convertedEth = ethers.formatEther(weiAmount); // wei â†’ ETH
console.log(weiAmount.toString(), "wei =", convertedEth, "ETH");

// å¤§æ•°å€¼è¿ç®—ï¼ˆé¿å…JSåŸç”Ÿè¿ç®—æº¢å‡ºï¼‰
const balance1 = ethers.parseEther("1.23");
const balance2 = ethers.parseEther("4.56");

const sum = balance1.add(balance2); // åŠ æ³•
const diff = balance2.sub(balance1); // å‡æ³•
const product = balance1.mul(2); // ä¹˜æ³•
const quotient = balance2.div(3); // é™¤æ³•

console.log("æ±‚å’Œï¼š", ethers.formatEther(sum), "ETH");
console.log("å·®å€¼ï¼š", ethers.formatEther(diff), "ETH");
```

## ä¸‰ã€ æ™ºèƒ½åˆçº¦äº¤äº’

### 1\. å‰æï¼šè·å– ABI ä¸åˆçº¦åœ°å€

-   **ABI è·å–**ï¼šä» Etherscan éªŒè¯åˆçº¦é¡µé¢å¤åˆ¶ï¼Œæˆ–ä» Hardhat ç¼–è¯‘åçš„`artifacts`æ–‡ä»¶å¤¹è¯»å–
    
-   **åˆçº¦åœ°å€**ï¼šéƒ¨ç½²åç”Ÿæˆçš„å”¯ä¸€åœ°å€ï¼ˆæµ‹è¯•ç½‘ / ä¸»ç½‘ï¼‰
    

### 2\. åˆçº¦è¯»å–æ“ä½œï¼ˆåªè¯»ï¼Œæ²¡æœ‰Gas æ¶ˆè€—ï¼‰

```
async function readContract() {
  // USDC Sepoliaæµ‹è¯•ç½‘åˆçº¦ä¿¡æ¯
  const usdcAddress = "0x1c7D4B196Cb0C7B01d743Fbc6116a902379C7238";
  const usdcAbi = [
    "function balanceOf(address owner) view returns (uint256)",
    "function decimals() view returns (uint8)",
    "function symbol() view returns (string)"
  ]; // ç®€åŒ–ABIï¼ˆä»…éœ€ç”¨åˆ°çš„å‡½æ•°ï¼‰

  // åˆå§‹åŒ–åªè¯»åˆçº¦å®ä¾‹
  const usdcContract = new ethers.Contract(usdcAddress, usdcAbi, infuraProvider);

  // è°ƒç”¨viewå‡½æ•°
  const symbol = await usdcContract.symbol();
  const decimals = await usdcContract.decimals();
  const balance = await usdcContract.balanceOf("0xd8dA6BF26964aF9D7eEd9e03E53415D37aA96045");

  console.log("ä»£å¸ç¬¦å·ï¼š", symbol);
  console.log("å°æ•°ä½æ•°ï¼š", decimals);
  console.log("é’±åŒ…ä½™é¢ï¼š", ethers.formatUnits(balance, decimals), symbol);
}

readContract();
```

### 3\. åˆçº¦å†™å…¥æ“ä½œï¼ˆäº¤æ˜“ï¼Œæ¶ˆè€— Gasï¼‰

3.1 ERC20 ä»£å¸è½¬è´¦ç¤ºä¾‹

js

```
async function writeContract() {
  const signer = await testWallet();
  const usdcAddress = "0x1c7D4B196Cb0C7B01d743Fbc6116a902379C7238";
  const usdcAbi = [
    "function transfer(address to, uint256 amount) returns (bool)",
    "function balanceOf(address owner) view returns (uint256)"
  ];

  // åˆå§‹åŒ–å¯å†™åˆçº¦å®ä¾‹ï¼ˆè¿æ¥Signerï¼‰
  const usdcContract = new ethers.Contract(usdcAddress, usdcAbi, signer);

  // è½¬è´¦å‚æ•°ï¼ˆè½¬10 USDCï¼Œæ³¨æ„å°æ•°ä½æ•°ï¼‰
  const recipient = "0xRecipientAddress";
  const amount = ethers.parseUnits("10", 6); // USDCå°æ•°ä½æ•°ä¸º6

  // å‘é€è½¬è´¦äº¤æ˜“
  const tx = await usdcContract.transfer(recipient, amount);
  console.log("è½¬è´¦äº¤æ˜“å“ˆå¸Œï¼š", tx.hash);
  const receipt = await tx.wait(1);
  if (receipt.status === 1) {
    console.log("è½¬è´¦æˆåŠŸï¼");
    // éªŒè¯ä½™é¢
    const newBalance = await usdcContract.balanceOf(recipient);
    console.log("æ¥æ”¶æ–¹æ–°ä½™é¢ï¼š", ethers.formatUnits(newBalance, 6), "USDC");
  }
}

writeContract();
```

### 4\. åŸå§‹äº¤æ˜“ä¸å‡½æ•°é€‰æ‹©å™¨

js

```
async function rawTransaction() {
  const signer = await testWallet();
  const contractAddress = "0xContractAddress";
  
  // 1. å‡½æ•°é€‰æ‹©å™¨ï¼štransfer(address,uint256)çš„å“ˆå¸Œå‰4å­—èŠ‚
  const functionSelector = ethers.id("transfer(address,uint256)").slice(0, 10);
  // 2. ç¼–ç å‚æ•°ï¼ˆæ¥æ”¶åœ°å€+è½¬è´¦é‡‘é¢ï¼‰
  const recipientEncoded = ethers.AbiCoder.defaultAbiCoder().encode(["address"], ["0xRecipientAddress"]);
  const amountEncoded = ethers.AbiCoder.defaultAbiCoder().encode(["uint256"], [ethers.parseUnits("10", 6)]);
  // 3. æ‹¼æ¥callData
  const callData = functionSelector + recipientEncoded.slice(2) + amountEncoded.slice(2);

  // å‘é€åŸå§‹äº¤æ˜“
  const tx = await signer.sendTransaction({
    to: contractAddress,
    data: callData
  });
  console.log("åŸå§‹äº¤æ˜“å“ˆå¸Œï¼š", tx.hash);
}
```

### 5\. äº¤æ˜“è¿›é˜¶æ–¹å‘ï¼šNonce ä¸ Gas ä¼˜åŒ–

js

```
async function optimizeTx() {
  const signer = await testWallet();
  // 1. è·å–è´¦æˆ·å½“å‰Nonce
  const nonce = await signer.getNonce("pending"); // pendingï¼šåŒ…å«å¾…ç¡®è®¤äº¤æ˜“
  // 2. è‡ªå®šä¹‰Gaså‚æ•°ï¼ˆåŠ é€Ÿäº¤æ˜“ï¼‰
  const gasPrice = (await infuraProvider.getGasPrice()).mul(120).div(100); // æé«˜20% Gas Price
  const gasLimit = 100000;

  const tx = await signer.sendTransaction({
    to: "0xRecipientAddress",
    value: ethers.parseEther("0.01"),
    nonce: nonce,
    gasPrice: gasPrice,
    gasLimit: gasLimit
  });
  console.log("è‡ªå®šä¹‰Gasäº¤æ˜“å“ˆå¸Œï¼š", tx.hash);
}
```

### 4\. æ ¸å¿ƒå®æˆ˜ï¼šéƒ¨ç½² + æµ‹è¯•ç¤ºä¾‹

4.1 ç¼–å†™ç®€å•åˆçº¦ï¼ˆcontracts/Counter.solï¼‰

solidity

```
// SPDX-License-Identifier: UNLICENSED
pragma solidity ^0.8.24;

contract Counter {
    uint256 public count;
    address public owner;

    constructor() {
        owner = msg.sender;
    }

    modifier onlyOwner() {
        require(msg.sender == owner, "Not owner");
        _;
    }

    function increment() public onlyOwner {
        count += 1;
    }

    function setCount(uint256 newCount) public onlyOwner {
        require(newCount >= 0, "Invalid count");
        count = newCount;
    }

    function getCount() public view returns (uint256) {
        return count;
    }
}
```

4.2 éƒ¨ç½²è„šæœ¬ï¼ˆscripts/deploy.jsï¼‰

js

```
import { ethers } from "hardhat";

async function main() {
  // éƒ¨ç½²åˆçº¦
  const Counter = await ethers.getContractFactory("Counter");
  const counter = await Counter.deploy();
  await counter.waitForDeployment();

  console.log(`Counteråˆçº¦éƒ¨ç½²åœ°å€ï¼š${await counter.getAddress()}`);

  // è°ƒç”¨åˆçº¦å‡½æ•°ï¼ˆéƒ¨ç½²åç«‹å³äº¤äº’ï¼‰
  await counter.increment();
  console.log("åˆå§‹è®¡æ•°ï¼š", await counter.getCount());
}

main().catch((error) => {
  console.error(error);
  process.exitCode = 1;
});
```

4.3 è‡ªåŠ¨åŒ–æµ‹è¯•ï¼ˆtest/counter-test.jsï¼‰

js

```
import { expect } from "chai";
import { ethers } from "hardhat";

describe("Counteråˆçº¦æµ‹è¯•", function () {
  let counter;
  let owner;
  let user;

  // æ¯ä¸ªæµ‹è¯•å‰éƒ¨ç½²æ–°åˆçº¦ï¼ˆéš”ç¦»ç¯å¢ƒï¼‰
  beforeEach(async function () {
    [owner, user] = await ethers.getSigners();
    const Counter = await ethers.getContractFactory("Counter");
    counter = await Counter.deploy();
    await counter.waitForDeployment();
  });

  // æµ‹è¯•1ï¼šåˆå§‹è®¡æ•°ä¸º0
  it("åˆå§‹è®¡æ•°åº”ä¸º0", async function () {
    expect(await counter.getCount()).to.equal(0);
  });

  // æµ‹è¯•2ï¼šæ‰€æœ‰è€…å¯å¢åŠ è®¡æ•°
  it("æ‰€æœ‰è€…å¯è°ƒç”¨increment", async function () {
    await counter.increment();
    expect(await counter.getCount()).to.equal(1);
  });

  // æµ‹è¯•3ï¼šéæ‰€æœ‰è€…ç¦æ­¢è°ƒç”¨increment
  it("éæ‰€æœ‰è€…è°ƒç”¨incrementåº”å¤±è´¥", async function () {
    await expect(counter.connect(user).increment()).to.be.revertedWith("Not owner");
  });
});
```

### 3\. åˆçº¦é—´äº¤äº’

solidity

```
// åˆçº¦Aï¼šBankï¼ˆå­˜å‚¨ETHï¼‰
contract Bank {
    mapping(address => uint256) public balances;
    address public owner;

    constructor() {
        owner = msg.sender;
    }

    function deposit() public payable {
        balances[msg.sender] += msg.value;
    }

    function withdraw(uint256 amount) public {
        require(balances[msg.sender] >= amount, "Insufficient balance");
        balances[msg.sender] -= amount;
        // å®‰å…¨è½¬è´¦ï¼šå…ˆæ›´æ–°çŠ¶æ€ï¼Œå†è½¬è´¦ï¼ˆé˜²é‡å…¥ï¼‰
        (bool success, ) = msg.sender.call{value: amount}("");
        require(success, "Transfer failed");
    }
}

// åˆçº¦Bï¼šMiddlewareï¼ˆè°ƒç”¨Bankåˆçº¦ï¼‰
contract Middleware {
    Bank public bank;

    constructor(address bankAddress) {
        bank = Bank(bankAddress);
    }

    // ä»£ç†å­˜æ¬¾
    function depositToBank() public payable {
        bank.deposit{value: msg.value}();
    }
}
```
